<script crossorigin="anonymous" integrity="sha256-Ls0pXSlb7AYs7evhd+VLnWsZ/AqEHcXBeMZUycz/CcA=" src="https://code.jquery.com/jquery-1.11.2.min.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
  	
  	$( document ).ready(function() {

                // GM remove op-0 class from footer to see chat GM
                $('.page-footer').removeClass('op-0');

  		var chatOptions = function(){


  		}


   		// Init
   		$(function(){

   			$.ajax({
				  url: "https://diwdev.info/sparchat/chat.php",
				  cache: false,
				  success: function(data){
  		$('#spk-chat').show('slow');
				    //console.log(data);
				    var chatMessage = $('#spk-chat-content');
				    var chatMenu = $('#spk-chat-menu');
				    for(var i = 0; i < data.menu.length; i++){
				    	//console.log(data.menu[i]);
				    	if(data.menu[i] !='Glavni meni'){
				    		chatMenu.append('<button type="button" class="spk-chat-menu-button" id="'+data.menu[i].id+'" data-menu-type="'+data.menu[i].menuType+'"> \
											'+data.menu[i].item+' \
							</button>');
				    	}
				    	else{
				    		// Create main menu button
				    		chatMenu.append('<button type="button" class="spk-chat-menu-button-home">Glavni meni</button>');
				    	}
				    }
	  	
				    	// create message
				    	chatMessage.append('<div class="talk-bubble tri-right left-top"><img src="/content/dam/ba/sba/common/chat/logo-veci.png" /><div class="talktext"><p class="chat-message">'+data.content+'</p></div></div>');

				    	
						setTimeout(recalculateHeights, 700);
				    	
				  }

			}); // End of Ajax init call;
				
		});

var amount;
var time;
var current;
   		$('body').on('click', '#spk-chat-menu button', function(e){	

   		// disable double click
   		$(this).prop('disabled', true);		     

            var clicked = e.currentTarget.dataset.menuType;
            if(e.currentTarget.id != 0 && clicked && clicked.indexOf('calculator_amount') == 0){
                amount = e.currentTarget.id;
                console.log('amount ',amount);
            }

            if(e.currentTarget.id != 0 && clicked && clicked.indexOf('calculator_period') == 0){

                time = e.currentTarget.id;
                console.log('time',time);
            }

				            /*console.log('menu', e.currentTarget.dataset.menuType);
				            console.log('amount', amount);
				            console.log('time', time);
				            console.log('e', e.currentTarget.innerText);*/

			            	$('#spk-chat-content').append('<div style="display: none;" class="talk-bubble tri-right right-top right-bubble"><div class="talktext"><p class="chat-message-right">'+e.currentTarget.innerText+'</p></div></div>');
                    $('#spk-chat-content').children().last('.talk-bubble').delay(700).fadeIn('slow');
							    	setTimeout(recalculateHeights, 500);

				$.ajax({
					  url: "https://diwdev.info/sparchat/chat.php",
					  type: 'POST',
					  data: { content:e.currentTarget.dataset.menuType, menu:e.currentTarget.dataset.menuType, amount:amount, time:time },
					  success: function(data) {
				           				           
						    var chatMessage = $('#spk-chat-content');
						    var chatMenu = $('#spk-chat-menu');
						    
						    chatMenu.empty();
						    
						    for(var i = 0; i < data.menu.length; i++){
						    	if(data.menu[i].item !='Glavni meni'){
						    		chatMenu.append('<button type="button" class="spk-chat-menu-button" id="'+data.menu[i].id+'" data-menu-type="'+data.menu[i].menuType+'"   data-amount="'+amount+'"> \
											'+data.menu[i].item+' \
															</button>');
						    	}
						    	else{

						    			chatMenu.append('<button type="button" class="spk-chat-menu-button-home" id="default" data-menu-type="default" >Glavni meni</button>');
						    	}
						    }
			  			    	chatMessage.append('<div  style="display: none;" class="talk-bubble tri-right left-top"><img src="/content/dam/ba/sba/common/chat/logo-veci.png" /><div class="talktext"><p class="chat-message">'+data.content+'<br /></p></div></div>');
                    chatMessage.children().last('.talk-bubble').delay(2000).fadeIn('slow');
                    setTimeout(recalculateHeights, 2010);

						    	current = e.currentTarget.dataset.menuType;
						    	if(current === 'default') {
						    		amount=null;
						    		time=null;
						    		chatMessage.children().not('.talk-bubble:first-child').remove();
						    	}
				        },
				        error: function(XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown) {
				            response = "err--" + XMLHttpRequest.status + " -- " + XMLHttpRequest.statusText;
				        }
					});
				})
   		
			$('#spk-chat').on('click', '#spk-chat-header', function() {
				$('#spk-chat').toggleClass('opened');
				$('#closeX').toggleClass('hidden');
				$('#openX').toggleClass('show');				
		    	var chatMessages = $('#spk-chat-content');
		    	var chatMenu = $('#spk-chat-menu');

				setTimeout(function() {
					setTimeout($('#spk-chat-body').toggleClass('opened'));
					recalculateHeights();
				}, 700);
			})
   	
	});

	function recalculateHeights() {
		var chat = $('#spk-chat');
		var chatHeader = $('#spk-chat-header');
	    var chatMessage = $('#spk-chat-content');
	    var chatMenu = $('#spk-chat-menu');
		chatMessage.height(chat.outerHeight() - chatMenu.outerHeight() - chatHeader.outerHeight());
//		chatMessage.scrollTo(0,chatMessage.scrollHeight);

    //    chatMessage.scrollTop( chatMessage.outerHeight() )

	    var scrollHeight = 0;
	    chatMessage.children().each(function(i, val) {
	      scrollHeight += $(val).outerHeight();
	    });

		chatMessage.animate({
		    scrollTop: scrollHeight
		  },
		    'slow')

	}
